### [237] [Bayesian Inference with Shaped Deep Non-linear MLPs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30860)
*Boris Hanin,Tianze Jiang*

Main category: math.ST

TL;DR: 本文研究深度非线性MLP在训练样本数、输入维度、隐藏层宽度和层数同时趋近于无穷时的贝叶斯推断，发现当LP/N处于Θ(1)量级时，存在一个简单的判据来判定深度是否有利于提升模型证据，并且预测后验等价于数据依赖的核方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度学习的理论需要刻画神经网络在大模型和大数据集同时存在时的预测行为，但由于模型参数和数据规模发散的顺序不交换，先验上不清楚存在哪些极限。本文旨在厘清这些极限问题。

Method: 基于神经协方差SDE框架，分析深度非线性MLP在P、N₀、N、L同时趋于无穷时的贝叶斯后验预测，聚焦LP/N∈Θ(1)的有效深度区域，涵盖光滑激活和ReLU激活，适用于任意温度。

Result: 发现在LP/N的一阶近似下，存在简单判据判断何种数据生成过程能从深度中获益（即更大的LP/N提升贝叶斯模型证据）；同时，贝叶斯预测后验等价于数据依赖的核方法。

Conclusion: 本文为深度贝叶斯推断提供了新见解，揭示了在特定极限下深度网络的后验预测具有惊人的简洁性，并为物理文献中的已有结果给出了新的推导。

Abstract: A central aim of deep learning theory is to characterize how neural networks make predictions in the regime of simultaneously large model and training set size. Since the limits of diverging number of model parameters and dataset size do not commute it is not clear a priori what limits exist. In this work, we shed new light on these questions by studying Bayesian inference in deep non-linear MLPs in the regime where the number of training samples ($P$), the input dimension ($N_0$), the hidden layer width ($N$), and the number of hidden layers ($L$) can all be large. We build on the Neural Covariance SDE (Li et al., 2022) to analyze predictive posteriors in the regime where $LP/N\inΘ(1)$, playing the role of an effective network depth. Our framework covers both smooth and ReLU activation functions and applies to arbitrary temperature. We find to first order in $LP/N$ a simple criterion for which data generating processes benefit from depth in the sense that larger $LP/N$ increases the Bayesian model evidence. We also give a novel derivation of a prior result from the physics literature that at least to first order in $LP/N$, the Bayesian predictive posterior is remarkably simple and is simply equivalent to that of a data-dependent kernel method.

### [238] [Improved Guarantees for Langevin Monte Carlo with Average Smoothness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31413)
*Arnak S. Dalalyan,Avetik Karagulyan*

Main category: math.ST

TL;DR: 本文建立了Langevin Monte Carlo在强对数凹设定下关于Wasserstein距离的非渐近界，其离散化误差由平均坐标-wise光滑常数而非全局光滑常数控制，并扩展到变步长、Laplacian光滑势能及有限和问题，在广义线性模型中展示了维度相关的显著改进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Langevin Monte Carlo的非渐近误差界依赖于全局Lipschitz光滑常数，这在高维问题中可能过于保守。作者希望建立更精细的误差界，通过利用坐标-wise的平均光滑性来获得更好的维度依赖关系。

Method: 采用同步耦合（synchronous coupling）的精细化版本进行概率分析，证明离散化误差由平均坐标-wise光滑常数控制。进一步将这一思想推广到变步长设定、Laplacian Lipschitz连续的势能（用迹型三阶光滑量替代Hessian-Lipschitz项）以及带固定点控制变量的随机梯度Langevin动力学（SGLD）的有限和问题。

Result: 新的非渐近界在全局光滑常数被平均坐标-wise光滑常数替代，在Laplacian光滑情形下Hessian-Lipschitz项被更弱的迹型三阶量替代，在SGLD中改进了对组件函数均方根光滑度的依赖。应用于高斯设计的广义线性模型时，特别是对于相关协变量，获得了维度依赖的实质性改进。

Conclusion: 通过更精细的耦合分析，证明了Langevin Monte Carlo的误差可用更弱的平均坐标-wise光滑常数控制，而非严格的全局光滑常数，这一改进在高维和相关协变量场景下尤为显著，且证明简洁而具有概率性。

Abstract: We establish improved nonasymptotic bounds for Langevin Monte Carlo in the strongly log-concave setting, when the error is measured by the Wasserstein distance. The main result shows that the discretization error is governed by an average coordinate-wise smoothness constant, rather than by the usual global smoothness constant. The proof is short and probabilistic, and relies on a refined use of the synchronous coupling. We further show that the same ideas lead to improved bounds for variable step sizes, for potentials whose Laplacian is Lipschitz-continuous, and for finite-sum problems sampled by stochastic-gradient Langevin dynamics with fixed point control variates. In the Laplacian-smooth case, the usual Hessian-Lipschitz contribution is replaced by a weaker trace-type third-order smoothness quantity. In the finite-sum setting, the resulting SGLD bound improves the dependence on the root mean square smoothness of the component functions. Applications to generalized linear models with Gaussian design show that these refinements can yield substantial, dimension-dependent improvements over previously known bounds, especially for correlated covariates.

</details>

### [239] [Investigating Detection and Obfuscation of Prompt Injection Attacks Against Software Reverse Engineering AI Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30677)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 智能体软件逆向工程系统容易受到可执行二进制文件源代码中嵌入的提示注入攻击，威胁其安全部署到生产级网络工作流中，因此需要深入理解相关风险并发展防御技术。

Method: 1) 检测反编译器输出中恶意示例程序的提示注入字符串；2) 探索提示注入攻击的混淆方法；3) 针对这些混淆提出相应的防御策略。

Result: 提出了针对反编译器输出中提示注入字符串的检测与防御机制，并验证了对混淆攻击的防御有效性。

Conclusion: 本研究推进了对智能体软件分析系统风险与安全性的理解，为将其部署到生产级网络工作流中提供了安全保障基础。

Abstract: Agentic software reverse engineering systems are vulnerable to prompt injection attacks placed into the source code of executable binary files. This research demonstrates defensive tactics for detecting the presences of prompt injection strings in the decompiler output of adversarial example programs. Methods for obfuscating these attacks and subsequent methods for defending against these obfuscations are also explored. This research advances the understanding of risk and security of agentic software analysis systems necessary for their deployment into production-level cyber workflows.

### [243] [Depth-Dependent Indirect Prompt Injection in Tool-Calling ReAct Agents: Injection Depth, Payload Framing, and Turn-Budget Sensitivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30686)
*Mohammadreza Rashidi*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了ReAct智能体在工具交互中面临的间接提示注入攻击风险，通过控制实验发现：注入深度是主导变量（第一轮工具观察捕获67%的攻击成功），而话语框架影响有限（中性25% vs 人格化75%），回合限制非风险因素。Claude Haiku在所有深度实现0%攻击成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准测试仅在固定注入位置和条件下评估攻击成功率，忽略了注入深度（工具序列中的位置）、修辞框架（话语风格）和回合限制三个风险维度，作者旨在系统探索这些未受关注的因素对间接提示注入攻击的影响。

Method: 在20个场景、5种攻击类别下进行四项控制研究，共460次试验，使用GPT-4o-mini和Claude Haiku，API总成本低于0.36美元。研究1: 变化注入深度(1-5)；研究2: 在Claude上复现深度实验；研究3: 变化话语框架(中性/指令/人格化等)；研究4: 变化回合限制(3/5/7)。

Result: (1) GPT-4o-mini的ASR从深度1的60%衰减至深度4-5的0%，Cramer's V=0.58；(2) Claude Haiku在所有深度均为0% ASR；(3) 框架在深度1产生25%-75%的ASR波动但统计不显著；(4) 回合限制对ASR无显著影响。

Conclusion: 注入深度是间接提示注入攻击的主导变量，安全防御应优先关注第一轮工具观测结果；不同模型对注入攻击的固有抵抗力差异显著（Claude Haiku优于GPT-4o-mini）；仅清理第一轮工具观测可捕获67%的注入成功案例。

Abstract: ReAct agents that interleave chain-of-thought reasoning with tool calls are increasingly deployed for real tasks such as scheduling, file retrieval, and data access. Their tool observation loop creates a direct attack surface: an adversary who controls any tool's return value can embed instructions that redirect the agent away from the user's goal, a threat known as indirect prompt injection. Existing benchmarks evaluate attack success rate (ASR) at a fixed injection position under fixed conditions, leaving three risk dimensions unexplored: where in the tool sequence the payload appears (injection depth), what rhetorical register it uses (framing), and how many turns the agent is permitted (turn cap). We conduct four controlled studies on 20 scenarios spanning five attack categories, totalling 460 trials against GPT-4o-mini and Claude Haiku at a combined API cost under 0.36 USD. Study 1 shows that ASR against GPT-4o-mini decays from 60% at depth 1 to 0% at depths 4 and 5 (Cramer's V = 0.58, p < 0.001; restricted to within-sequence depths 1-3: V = 0.47, p = 0.0013), driven by model resistance at depth 1 and task completion before payload encounter at deeper positions. Study 2 replicates the depth experiment on Claude Haiku, which achieves 0% ASR at every depth through a combination of conservative tool invocation and genuine instruction resistance. Study 3 shows that framing modulates ASR between 25% (neutral) and 75% (persona) at depth 1, a 50-percentage-point range that does not reach statistical significance at N = 20 per condition. Study 4 confirms that ASR is stable across turn caps of 3, 5, and 7, indicating the turn budget is not a risk factor in this setting. Our results establish injection depth as the dominant variable and show that sanitising only the first tool observation captures 67% of measured injection successes.

Method: 基于Bradley-Terry偏好模型和成对偏好数据的内在几何结构，从私有数据中学习带有差分隐私保证的偏好模型，再利用该模型结合公共提示合成高质量偏好数据。通过聚类奖励模型的共享线性结构和DP-PCA提高学习精度。

To address this, we propose DPPrefSyn, a novel algorithm for generating differentially private (DP) synthetic preference data to enable privacy-preserving preference alignment. DPPrefSyn is a principled framework grounded in the Bradley-Terry preference model and the intrinsic geometric structure of pairwise human preference data. It first learns an underlying preference model from private data with formal differential privacy guarantees, and then leverages the learned model together with public prompts to synthesize high-quality preference data. It exploits the shared linear structure of per-cluster reward models to effectively capture heterogeneous human preferences in private datasets, and leverages DP Principal Component Analysis (DP-PCA) to improve learning accuracy. Extensive experimental results demonstrate that DPPrefSyn achieves competitive alignment performance under strong DP guarantees. These findings highlight the potential of synthetic preference data as a practical alternative for privacy-preserving preference alignment across a broad range of applications. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first work to generate DP synthetic preference data for LLM alignment. Our code is available at https://github.com/gfengyu/Differentially-Private-Preference-Data-Synthesis.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: SCOUT框架将检测重构为检测器分配问题：针对每个请求，根据历史行为预测各检测器的样本级可靠性和延迟，动态决定运行哪些检测器以及是否升级到LLM裁判，并通过单一安全-效用阈值供操作员调节。

Abstract: Prompt-injection detectors are heterogeneous: each is strong on a different slice of attacks, and none is always reliable. Yet existing systems still treat detection as a fixed single-detector pipeline, committing every request to one detector's blind spots. We reframe defense as detector allocation: given a heterogeneous pool, decide per request which detectors to run and whether to escalate to an LLM judge. Our framework SCOUT (Scalable and Controllable Outcome-prediction for Uncertainty-aware Triage) makes this decision dynamic by predicting each detector's per-sample reliability and latency from how it behaved on similar past inputs, and exposes a single safety-utility threshold to the operator (where utility bundles benign-pass rate and wall-clock). To evaluate this setting, we build SCOUT-450, a benchmark that captures the structurally complex, agent-facing injections that older prompt-injection sets under-represent. On SCOUT-450, a safety-oriented operating point reduces attack-success rate by 46% and total wall-clock by 40% relative to an always-on GPT-4o judge, at a 5.1-point benign-utility drop. SCOUT also transfers to three external benchmarks (BIPIA, IPI, and IHEval), improving the safety-utility frontier.

  <summary>Details</summary>

### [247] [ZAPS-DA: Zero-Phase Action Policy Smoothing with Decoupled Actor for Continuous Control in Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30612)
*Faiq Shamass*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: ZAPS-DA通过解耦的模仿学习策略，在不引入相位延迟和后处理的情况下，将强化学习策略的动作抖动降低14-45倍，同时保持任务性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 离线强化学习策略在物理部署时存在高频动作抖动问题，现有后处理方法引入相位延迟，而嵌入平滑惩罚会与RL梯度耦合，导致过度平滑与奖励回归之间的冲突。

Method: ZAPS-DA框架：主策略保持原始RL训练不变，解耦策略通过监督学习模仿重放缓冲区中经零相位滤波处理的目标动作，实现非因果滤波器的因果蒸馏。采用幅度匹配的MSE损失实现零超参数迁移。

Result: 在MetaDrive中：转向抖动降低14-21倍，油门抖动降低3-5倍（p<10^-4），任务完成率无显著差异（p=0.28成功率，p=0.31碰撞率），奖励成本6.3%。在Webots中：帕累托改进，转向抖动降低8-45倍，任务失败率从2.0%降至0.7%，奖励无显著差异（p=0.121）。

Conclusion: ZAPS-DA能有效消除RL策略的动作抖动，无需后处理且相位延迟可忽略，在不同环境和优化器下均表现稳健，为RL策略的物理部署提供了一种实用解决方案。

Abstract: Continuous control policies trained with off-policy reinforcement learning frequently exhibit high-frequency action jitter, rendering direct deployment on physical actuators impractical. Post-hoc filtering attenuates jitter but introduces phase lag; embedding smoothness penalties in the actor's loss couples them with the RL gradient and conflates reward regression with over-aggressive smoothing. We present ZAPS-DA, a framework that reduces action jitter at deployment with negligible phase lag and no post-processing. ZAPS-DA pairs an unmodified main actor (trained by the base RL loss) with a separate decoupled actor trained via supervised imitation of zero-phase filtered targets stored in the replay buffer. The deployed policy is the decoupled actor: a feed-forward map from the current observation to a smooth action, with no inference-time filter and no action-history input -- a mechanism we term causal distillation of a non-causal filter. A magnitude-matched MSE loss provides zero-hyperparameter portability across optimizer classes. Validated with Soft Actor-Critic and a Savitzky--Golay filter in two driving simulators using paired n=150 evaluation protocols: on MetaDrive, ZAPS-DA reduces steering jitter by 14--21x and throttle jitter by 3--5x (all $p < 10^{-4}$, Bonferroni-corrected) while matching task-completion (p=0.28 success, p=0.31 crash) at a 6.3% reward cost; on a custom Webots adaptive cruise control environment, the same SG configuration produces a Pareto improvement -- reward parity (p=0.121), 8--45x steering jitter reduction, and total task-failure rate reduced from 2.0% to 0.7%.

</details>


### [248] [Don't Fool Me Twice: Adapting to Adversity in the Wild with Experience-Driven Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31119)
*Navin Sriram Ravie,Andrew Jong,Krrish Jain,John Liu,Omar Alama,Bijo Sebastian,Sebastian Scherer*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 提出持续学习框架"Don't Fool Me Twice"，让移动机器人在线学习 disturbances，通过语义归因异常行为，实现未知非结构化环境下的自主适应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在未知非结构化环境中，难以预先预测所有针对具体机器人的危险和对抗模式，现有的VLM方法无法捕捉交互依赖和具身相关的 adversities。

Method: 1) 观察 disturbances 并描述效果；2) 结合视觉上下文查询VLM预测可能原因；3) 使用核回归对局部 disturbance 进行小样本瞬态异常建模；4) 基于语义体素中心建模估计认知不确定性，将交互驱动的 disturbances 作为可学习空间行为。

Result: 在仿真和硬件平台上跨具身形态和对抗模式进行了验证，支持提出的四个假设。

Conclusion: 通过在线学习 disturbances 并进行语义归因，机器人能更好地预测和规划未来行为，实现未知环境下的鲁棒自主操作。

Abstract: In robotics, dangers and adversity modes are often embodiment-specific and relative to each agent. A frontier of autonomous mobile robotics is to enable agents to operate effectively in the wild in unseen unstructured environments. A significant challenge in unseen unstructured environments is that it may not be possible to predict all the dangers to the specific robot. Although recent work has used large foundation vision-language models (VLMs) to preemptively predict an exhaustive list of common-sense dangers, it remains difficult to capture possible interaction and embodiment-dependent adversities. We propose a continual learning framework for a mobile embodied agent to learn online from disturbances and attribute anomalous behaviours to causes through semantics, enabling better prediction and planning of the world in the future. Our framework, "Don't Fool Me Twice", first observes disturbances and describes their effects on the robot; this description is augmented with visual context to query a VLM to predict possible causes; the local disturbance is characterized using kernel regression, which allows for efficient, few-shot modeling of transient anomalies. We leverage semantic voxel-centric modeling to estimate epistemic uncertainty, enabling richer downstream recovery by treating interaction-driven disturbances as learnable spatial behaviors. We present four hypotheses and validate them in simulation and on hardware across embodiments and adversity modes.

</details>

### [249] [Discovering Thermodynamically Admissible Dissipation Potentials via Grammar-Based Symbolic Regression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31532)
*Federico Califano,Jacopo Ciambella*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 提出了一种符号回归框架，用于在广义标准材料（GSM）框架下自动发现满足热力学约束（凸性和非负性）的耗散势函数，并通过合成数据和实验数据验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的数据驱动方法虽然能保证热力学相容性，但牺牲了可解释性。作者希望提出一种既能保证热力学严格性又能保持可解释性的符号回归方法。

Method: 基于Clausius-Duhem不等式，在广义标准材料（GSM）框架下，通过扩展凸性保持语法生成候选耗散势函数，确保凸性和非负性条件自动满足，涵盖率相关（粘弹性）和粘塑性耗散机制。

Result: 在牛顿、幂律、Bingham粘塑性等合成数据集上验证有效，并在合成弹性体的实验振荡剪切测试中，发现了能复现振幅相关软化行为的耗散势，优于校准的线性Zener基线模型。

Conclusion: 所提出的符号回归框架能够在保证热力学严格性的同时，自动发现具有可解释性的耗散势，为数据驱动本构建模提供了一种兼顾精度与可解释性的方案。

Abstract: Constitutive laws for inelastic materials must satisfy strict thermodynamic admissibility requirements, yet current data-driven approaches sacrifice interpretability, even when formal guarantees are provided by physics-encoded architectures. We propose a symbolic regression framework for the data-driven discovery of dissipation potentials governing the evolution of internal variables within the Generalized Standard Materials (GSM) formalism. Starting from the Clausius--Duhem inequality, we enforce the thermodynamic requirements, convexity and non-negativity, that the dual dissipation potential must satisfy to guarantee non-negative mechanical dissipation. These requirements are formulated in the general subdifferential setting, encompassing rate-dependent (viscoelastic) and viscoplastic dissipative mechanisms, including potentials with genuine elastic domains, within a unified framework. Candidate potentials are generated by a composition-extended convexity-preserving grammar that guarantees thermodynamic admissibility \emph{by construction}. The framework is validated on synthetic datasets spanning Newtonian, power-law, and Bingham viscoplastic ground truths under process and measurement noise, and on experimental oscillatory shear measurements of a synthetic elastomer across multiple strain amplitudes and frequencies, where the discovered potentials reproduce the amplitude-dependent softening of the dynamic moduli and outperform a calibrated linear Zener baseline.

</details>

### [250] [Enhancing Regime Shift Detection Using Unstructured Data: A Study on the Treasury Market](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30363)
*Mingxuan Yi,Vidal Mehra,Jing Chen,John Cartlidge*

Main category: q-fin.CP

TL;DR: 论文提出了一种结合大语言模型推理和统计检验的文本增强型金融制度转换检测框架，在2010-2024年FOMC会议记录和14维宏观金融数据上取得了F1=0.82的性能，优于纯数据驱动基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 金融市场中的制度转换难以被纯数据驱动方法可靠检测，因为数据信号噪声大、多重共线性强，而政策沟通文本往往在价格变化之前就发出了信号，但现有方法忽视了这些非结构化文本信息。

Method: 提出一个检测器无关的双向验证框架：1) 用LLM从央行沟通文本中提取候选制度转换点，再用VAR的bootstrap似然比检验进行统计验证；2) 数据驱动检测器发现的候选点，通过LLM文本检查进行确认。使用了四种可替代的数据驱动检测器。

Result: 在2010-2024年FOMC会议记录和14变量美国国债与宏观经济面板数据上，该框架达到F1=0.82，当日检测中位数延迟，一致优于纯数据驱动基线方法。

Conclusion: 将非结构化政策文本与统计结构断点检测相结合，能够提高金融市场制度转换识别的鲁棒性和可解释性。

Abstract: Regime shifts in financial markets reorganise the joint dynamics of asset prices and macro variables, breaking any single-regime calibration. They are nonetheless difficult to detect reliably because the data signal is noisy and heavily multicollinear, while the contemporaneous text that announces them is unstructured. Standard regime shift detection methods rely solely on structured time-series data and ignore policy communications, even though these texts often signal shifts before they materialise in observed prices. We propose a text-enhanced regime shift detection pipeline that combines large language model (LLM) reasoning over central-bank communications with statistical validation on multivariate financial time series. The framework is detector-agnostic: text-proposed candidates are validated using a bootstrap likelihood-ratio test on a vector autoregression (VAR), while data-driven candidates from arbitrary regime detectors are ratified through a lenient LLM text check. We evaluate the framework on 2010-2024 FOMC minutes paired with a 14-variable U.S. Treasury and macroeconomic panel, using four interchangeable data-driven detectors. The proposed pipeline achieves F1 = 0.82 against a verified anchor list of monetary-policy regime shifts, with same-day modal detection latency and consistently stronger performance than pure data-driven baselines. The results demonstrate that combining unstructured policy text with statistical structural-break detection improves the robustness and interpretability of regime shift identification in financial markets.

</details>

### [251] [Contextual Scalarisation Thompson Sampling for multi-objective decisions in public media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31291)
*Théo Maëtz,Luc Guillet,Andrea Cavallaro*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 提出Contextual Scalarisation Thompson Sampler (CSTS)，一种能根据上下文动态学习目标权重的多目标上下文bandit方法，在瑞士广播公司真实数据上表现优于固定权重方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 推荐系统常需平衡多个竞争目标（如受众覆盖、文化价值、公共任务等），现有方法使用固定权重组合或Pareto优化，无法适应不同情境下优先级的变化。

Method: 提出CSTS（Contextual Scalarisation Thompson Sampler），一种多目标上下文bandit方法，能够根据观察到的上下文信息动态学习各目标的权重。

Result: 在Radio Télévision Suisse的真实节目编排数据上评估，CSTS相比固定权重和标准上下文bandit方法，展现了更好的上下文相关性和与专家策展实践的一致性。

Conclusion: CSTS通过上下文感知的动态目标加权，有效解决了多目标推荐中优先级随情境变化的问题，在实际公共媒体数据中验证了其有效性。

Abstract: Recommender systems may operate under multiple, competing objectives. For example, audience reach, cultural values, public service mandate, and operational constraints must be balanced in editorial decisions of public service media. Existing approaches relying on fixed combinations of objectives or Pareto-based optimisation do not adapt to changing priorities across situations. In this paper, we propose Contextual Scalarisation Thompson Sampler (CSTS), a multi-objective contextual bandit method that learns to weight objectives as a function of the observed context. We evaluate CSTS on real programming data from Radio Télévision Suisse, the Swiss national broadcaster, showing improved contextual relevance and better alignment with expert curation practices compared to fixed weight and standard contextual bandit approaches.

</details>

Abstract: Generative machine learning has become an essential tool in theoretical and experimental physics, especially in the context of fast surrogates and density estimators. ### [253] [Learning effective Sargassum transport dynamics from limited drifter observations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30603)
*F. J. Beron-VEra,M. J. Olascoaga,J. Morell,E. Cruz*

Main category: physics.ao-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一个数据驱动的传输学习框架，利用有限拉格朗日观测数据和物理启发的大气-海洋诊断量，对漂浮物输运进行有效校正。在波多黎各和墨西哥湾流区域的马尾藻漂流器数据上验证，发现诊断量包含基线环流产品之外的输运相关信息，且不同流态下延迟记忆效应表现不同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 漂浮物输运受到未解析过程的影响，而这些过程通常不在现有环流产品中体现，需要从有限观测中学习有效的输运校正。

Method: 构建数据驱动的传输学习框架，采用物理启发的大气-海洋诊断量、有限记忆表征（惯性粒子记忆效应）、MLP集成进行轨迹校正，以及SINDy进行稀疏符号发现。

Result: 波多黎各区域：延迟稀疏符号校正有适度但系统性的提升；墨西哥湾流区域：动态有用的稀疏符号校正主要是瞬时的，尽管延迟预测信息存在。

Conclusion: 支持粗粒度漂浮物输运中存在有限记忆效应，同时表明获取稳定的延迟稀疏符号闭合具有一定难度。

Abstract: Floating-material transport is influenced by unresolved processes that are often absent from available circulation products. We develop a data-driven transport-learning framework for learning effective transport corrections from limited Lagrangian observations using physically motivated ocean--atmosphere diagnostics and finite-memory representations motivated in part by inertial-particle memory effects. The diagnostic representation is analyzed through predictive and sparse symbolic-discovery approaches under leave-one-trajectory-out validation. Applications to Sargassum-following drifters in the Puerto Rico region and the Gulf Stream show that the diagnostics contain transport-relevant information beyond the baseline circulation products. Multilayer perceptron (MLP) ensembles provide flexible predictive trajectory corrections, while Sparse Identification of Nonlinear Dynamics (SINDy) tests whether instantaneous or delayed sparse symbolic transport structure can be extracted from the diagnostics. The results differ across flow regimes: (i) in Puerto Rico, delayed sparse symbolic corrections provide modest but systematic improvement; (ii) in the Gulf Stream application, dynamically useful sparse symbolic corrections remain primarily instantaneous even though delayed predictive information persists. These results support finite-memory transport effects in coarse-grained floating-material transport while also illustrating the difficulty of obtaining stable delayed sparse symbolic closures.

</details>

### [254] [Incremental BPE Tokenization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30813)
*Shenghu Jiang,Ruihao Gong*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出了一种增量式BPE分词算法，最坏情况下每个字节处理时间为O(log² t)，整体复杂度O(n log² t)，相比Hugging Face实现加速约3倍，并支持流式输出。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准BPE分词在流式场景下效率低下，缺乏增量维护分词结果的算法，导致无法高效处理部分输入或流式数据。

Method: 提出增量式BPE算法，每个输入字节最坏O(log² t)时间处理，维护每个前缀的BPE分词结果；另提出eager output算法，在增量过程中一旦确定token边界立即输出，支持流式输出。

Result: 相比Hugging Face tokenizers加速约3倍；在病态输入上相比OpenAI tiktoken显著降低延迟；具有强最坏情况保证。

Conclusion: BPE分词可以在具有强最坏情况保证下增量执行，并在现代LLM管线中带来实际延迟收益。

Abstract: We propose a novel algorithm for incremental Byte Pair Encoding (BPE) tokenization. The algorithm processes each input byte in worst-case $\mathcal{O}(\log^2 t)$ time, leading to an overall complexity of $\mathcal{O}(n \log^2 t)$, where $n$ is the input length and $t$ is the maximum token length. The algorithm incrementally maintains BPE tokenization results for every prefix of the input text, implementing the standard BPE merge procedure defined by a fixed set of merge rules. This enables efficient partial tokenization in streaming settings. Functioning as a drop-in replacement for standard BPE, our approach achieves a speedup of up to ${\sim}3\times$ over Hugging Face's tokenizers, and demonstrates significant latency reductions over OpenAI's tiktoken on pathological inputs. We further introduce an eager output algorithm that enables streaming output, emitting tokens as soon as token boundaries are determined during incremental tokenization. Overall, our results demonstrate that BPE tokenization can be performed incrementally with strong worst-case guarantees, while providing practical latency benefits in modern large language model pipelines. Code: https://github.com/ModelTC/mtc-inc-bpe

</details>


### [255] [Neuro-symbolic Syntactic Parsing: Shaping a Neural Network with the CYK Algorithm](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31421)
*Fabio Massimo Zanzotto,Federico Ranaldi,Giorgio Satta*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出CYKNN架构，将CYK解析算法直接注入循环神经网络，通过可训练的矩阵-向量乘法实现算法编码，在简单文法任务上超越大型语言模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索将复杂算法直接注入神经网络架构的可能性，挑战纯数据驱动的深度学习方法，为神经符号系统提供新思路。

Method: 设计CYKNN——一种编码CYK算法（Chomsky范式的上下文无关文法解析算法）的简单循环神经网络架构，将算法步骤转化为可训练的矩阵-向量乘法运算。

Result: 在4种变体的简单文法实验中，CYKNN超越了超过200亿参数的LLM（上下文学习设置）以及Qwen系列（LoRA微调）的小型语言模型。

Conclusion: 证明了算法直接注入神经网络的可行性，为神经符号方法论开辟了全新路径。

Abstract: In this paper, we show the possibility of a direct injection of algorithms into neural network architecture. We focus on a complex algorithm, that is, Cocke-Youger-Kasami (CYK) for parsing context-free grammars in Chomsky Normal Form and we propose CYKNN, a simple recurrent neural network architecture for encoding the CYK algorithm in trainable matrix-vector multiplications.We experimented with a very simple grammar with 4 variations showing that our approach outperforms existing LLMs with more than 20B parameters with an in-context learning setting and smaller LLMs of the Qwen family fine-tuned with LoRA. Our attempt paves the way to a different approach to neuro-symbolic methodologies.

</details>


### [256] [Combinatorial Synthesis: Scaling Code RLVR via Atomic Decomposition and Recombination](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31058)
*Jiasheng Zheng,Boxi Cao,Boxi Yu,Yuzhong Zhang,Jialun Cao,Yaojie Lu,Hongyu Lin,Xianpei Han,Le Sun*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出原子分解与重组（ADR）框架，通过将代码任务分解为原子元素并受控重组，生成新颖且具挑战性的可验证代码任务，从而解决RLVR中高质量训练数据稀缺的问题。实验表明ADR在原创性、难度、多样性和测试质量上优于现有方法，并能持续提升LLM在多领域（算法编程、工具使用、数据科学）的代码能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RLVR方法受限于可验证代码任务的稀缺性，尤其是缺乏足够挑战性、接近模型能力边缘的任务。以往依赖启发式种子扩展的数据合成方法在创新性和难度上严重受限，导致训练数据的价值无法随合成规模成正比增长。

Method: 提出原子分解与重组（ADR）框架：将复杂代码任务分解为不可再分的原子元素，再通过受控重组生成全新且难度可控的可验证代码任务，确保任务的新颖性和挑战性。

Result: ADR在原创性、难度、多样性和测试质量上均优于现有基线；在算法编程、工具使用、数据科学等多个下游领域的RLVR训练中，持续带来更显著的代码能力提升。

Conclusion: ADR为新颖代码任务合成和可扩展的RLVR训练提供了新范式，表明通过结构化分解与重组可以突破数据稀缺瓶颈，实现训练数据价值随规模增长。

Abstract: Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has recently emerged as the cornerstone for shaping the remarkable coding abilities of Large Language Models (LLMs). However, the scalability of RLVR is severely constrained by the scarcity of sufficiently challenging verifiable code tasks that target near the model's edge of competence. Prior studies often rely on heuristic seed expansions for data synthesis, which severely limits both novelty and difficulty. Consequently, the training value of such data fails to scale proportionally with the size of its synthesis. To this end, we propose Atomic Decomposition and Recombination (ADR), a novel framework that generates verifiable code tasks via decomposition into atomic elements and controlled recombination, thereby enabling the generation of genuinely novel and challenging verifiable code tasks. Experiments and analysis demonstrate that ADR achieves superior originality, difficulty, diversity, and test quality over existing baselines, and consistently delivers greater improvements in code ability across RLVR in diverse downstream domains, including algorithmic programming, tool usage, and data science. Our work sheds light on a new paradigm for novel code task synthesis and scalable RLVR training.

### [257] [Exploring Autonomous Agentic Data Engineering for Model Specialization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30407)
*Yujie Luo,Xiangyuan Ru,Jingsheng Zheng,Jingjing Wang,Yuqi Zhu,Jintian Zhang,Runnan Fang,Kewei Xu,Ye Liu,Zheng Wei,Jiang Bian,Zang Li,Shumin Deng*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出自主代理数据工程（Autonomous Agentic Data Engineering）这一新任务，让LLM作为自主数据工程师，通过端到端数据策划驱动模型专业化。实验表明，GPT-5.2自主构建训练课程使模型性能提升57.29%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM数据筛选方法依赖人工设计的工作流，未探索LLM能否自主执行完整的数据工程流程来实现模型专业化。

Method: 将数据视为可优化组件，设计智能体自主规划、生成并迭代优化训练数据，以模型训练后的性能提升为导向，跨多个领域进行数据策展。

Result: GPT-5.2自主构建训练课程，使学生模型性能提升57.29%，完全通过迭代的智能体驱动数据适应实现。

Conclusion: 自主数据工程是一种可衡量的能力，为智能体驱动的模型专业化指明了方向。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have demonstrated strong performance on general tasks, while often struggling to adapt to specialized domains without high-quality domain-specific data. Existing LLM-based data curation methods primarily rely on human-designed workflows, leaving it unexamined whether LLMs can autonomously execute an end-to-end data engineering pipeline for model specialization. We formalize \textbf{Autonomous Agentic Data Engineering}, a novel task designed to evaluate LLMs as autonomous data engineers that drive model specialization through end-to-end data curation. We frame data as an optimizable component and study agents that plan, generate, and iteratively optimize training data across multiple domains, guided by post-training performance improvement. Experiments show that autonomous LLM data engineers yield substantial gains, as GPT-5.2 constructs a training curriculum that improves a student model by \textbf{57.29\%}, entirely through iterative, agent-driven data adaptation. By illuminating both potential and bottlenecks, our study establishes autonomous data engineering as a measurable capability and charts a path toward agent-driven model specialization\footnote{Code will be released at https://github.com/zjunlp/DataAgent.}.

### [258] [Generalistic or Specific Embeddings, Which is Better? An Empirical Study on Search for Clinical Coding in Non-English Languages](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30529)
*David Rey-Blanco,Roberto Cruz*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出利用大型生成语言模型（Gemini）生成多语言合成数据（英、西、加泰、意、葡、法），微调西班牙生物医学编码器构建两阶段检索器（bi-encoder + cross-encoder reranker），在ICD-10-CM/CIE-10代码检索任务上显著提升非英语语言（尤其葡萄牙语R@5从0.714提升至0.829），仅以小幅英语性能回撤为代价。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 句子嵌入模型在语义搜索中主要基于英语语料开发和评估，当应用于其他语言的临床检索（特别是ICD-10-CM/CIE-10代码检索）时，召回率下降且被聚合基准掩盖。作者试图探究大型生成语言模型能否作为数据工厂来弥合这一差距。

Method: 构建两阶段检索器：bi-encoder（候选检索）+ cross-encoder（重排器）。在西班牙生物医学编码器（PlanTL-GOB-ES/bsc-bio-ehr-es）基础上，使用Gemini生成的约19,500条多语言（英、西、加泰、意、葡、法）合成数据进行微调，并与BioBERT-ST及未微调的西班牙编码器进行对比评估。

Result: 仅bi-encoder在MRR（0.876 vs 0.866）、R@3（0.650 vs 0.626）和R@5（0.804 vs 0.790）上超越BioBERT-ST。加入cross-encoder重排器后，聚合R@5提升至0.822，在四种非英语语言上占优（西+0.017、加泰+0.033、法+0.018、葡+0.037），英语略有回撤。葡萄牙语R@5达0.829（BioBERT-ST仅0.714）。MRR从0.755提升至0.876（+15.9%）。

Conclusion: 本文贡献：1）基于LLM生成数据构建领域特定医学检索器的开源方案；2）量化了学习增益（约19,500条合成对带来MRR+15.9%）；3）按语言和排名位置刻画了性能提升的分布。验证了生成式LLM作为数据工厂在低资源临床检索场景的有效性。

Abstract: Sentence-embedding models for semantic search are overwhelmingly developed and evaluated on English corpora. When applied to clinical retrieval in other languages -- particularly retrieval of ICD-10-CM / CIE-10 codes -- recall degrades in ways often masked by aggregate benchmarks. We study whether large generative language models can serve as data factories to close this gap. We build a two-stage retriever (bi-encoder followed by cross-encoder reranker), fine-tuned from a Spanish biomedical encoder (PlanTL-GOB-ES/bsc-bio-ehr-es) on Gemini-generated synthetic data covering English, Spanish, Catalan, Italian, Portuguese and French, and evaluate against BioBERT-ST and the un-tuned Spanish encoder. The bi-encoder alone matches BioBERT-ST on MRR (0.876 vs. 0.866) and overtakes it on R@3 (0.650 vs. 0.626) and R@5 (0.804 vs. 0.790) without English biomedical pretraining. Adding a cross-encoder reranker lifts aggregate R@5 to 0.822 and dominates on four of five languages (+0.017 Spanish, +0.033 Catalan, +0.018 French, +0.037 Portuguese) at the cost of a small English regression. The trade-off is clinically acceptable: Portuguese reaches R@5 = 0.829 vs. BioBERT-ST's 0.714. Contributions: an open recipe for building domain-specific medical retrievers from LLM-generated data; quantification of the learning gain (MRR 0.755 to 0.876, +15.9% with ~19,500 synthetic pairs); and a characterisation of where gains concentrate by language and rank.

</details>


### [259] [Speculative Decoding Across Languages](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30580)
*Nirajan Paudel,Michael Ginn,Luc De Nardi,Alexis Palmer*

TL;DR: 针对非英语语言中推测解码效率低的问题，本文比较了三种改进策略：微调任务专用数据、微调单语语料库、训练n-gram草稿模型。发现任务专用蒸馏虽能提升效率但泛化差，而n-gram模型尽管接受率较低，但因生成速度快而持续带来较大加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型推理中，推测解码通过草稿-验证并行机制加速生成，但小型草稿模型在多语言能力上存在严重不足，导致非英语文本生成时推测解码效率大幅下降。

Method: 对11种语言比较三种策略：1) 在任务特定数据（翻译）上微调草稿模型；2) 在无标签单语语料上微调草稿模型；3) 在相同单语语料上训练简单n-gram草稿模型。在翻译（英译目标语言）和故事生成任务上评估效率。

Result: 任务专用蒸馏能显著提升效率，但蒸馏模型在新任务上泛化能力差；n-gram草稿模型虽然接受率较低，但由于草稿生成速度极快，始终能提供大幅加速。

Conclusion: 在非英语语言的推测解码中，简单的n-gram草稿模型因生成速度快，在实践中比复杂的蒸馏微调策略更具优势，尤其当需要跨任务泛化时。

Abstract: Speculative decoding has become a crucial component of large language model (LLM) inference, enabling faster generation by drafting multiple tokens and verifying them in parallel. However, small draft models tend to suffer from disproportionately poor multilingual capabilities. Thus, when generating text in a non-English language, speculative decoding is far less effective.
  We compare three strategies to improve speculative decoding efficiency for eleven languages: finetuning the draft model on task-specific data (translation); finetuning the draft model on unlabeled monolingual corpora; and training simple n-gram draft models on the same monolingual corpora. We evaluate efficiency on translation (from English into the target language) and the held-out task of story generation. We find that while task-specific distillation can significantly improve efficiency, distilled models generalize poorly to a new task. Meanwhile, n-gram draft models, despite lower acceptance rates, consistently provide large speed-ups due to much faster draft generation.

### [260] [The Architecture of Errors: From Universal Impossibility to Patch-Local LLM Reliability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30628)
*Mikhail L. Arbuzov,Lee Mosbacker,Sisong Bei,Ziwei Dong,Dmitri Kalaev,Alexey Shvets*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文论证了大语言模型在通用场景下不存在有限的失败模式字典，但在操作有界的具体领域（如法律审查、医疗RAG等）中，失败模式稀疏且重复，可靠性问题可转化为局部目录发现与干预覆盖问题。通过两个命题和一个推论形式化了这一转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型的可靠性在理论上无界（失败模式无限增长），但在实际部署中系统运行于操作有界的领域内。现有研究多关注通用失败模式，缺乏对局部域内失败模式稀疏性、重复性的形式化刻画及相应的可靠性保证框架。

Method: 提出两个命题和一个推论：(1) Proposition 1：无界域中无有限干预字典可覆盖所有可区分的失败模式（最坏情况负向结果）；(2) Corollary 1：失败模式发现的指数级困难——对数上界无法在线性增长下容忍更多尾部模式；(3) Proposition 2：在局部域中，给定对数级活跃模式暴露和头部重覆盖，每个硬决策的干预预算随序列长度呈多对数增长，域目录饱和后趋于常数。

Result: 建立了从通用无界可靠性问题到局部目录发现问题的理论转化框架：在操作有界的域中，可靠性成本从指数级降为多对数级乃至常数；但困难并未消失——当硬决策数量随任务长度增长时，可靠性依然困难，该框架的作用是正确定位干预轴心。

Conclusion: 大语言模型的可靠性问题需要区分域内（可缓解）与跨域（固有困难）两个层次；未来应聚焦于特定操作域内的目录发现与覆盖策略，而非追求通用的无界可靠性保证。

Abstract: Universal LLM reliability is not a finite-library problem: across all possible tasks, tools, schemas, knowledge sources, and evaluator expectations, new intervention-distinguishable failure modes can appear without bound, so no finite intervention dictionary can guarantee bounded residual error for every such mode. But deployed systems do not operate over the whole universe. They operate inside operationally bounded patches (legal review, medical RAG, code repair, customer-support agents, contract extraction) with recurring tasks, schemas, tools, and evaluator expectations. Within such patches, empirical evidence suggests failures are sparse, repetitive, and concentrated in a small recurring catalogue, so reliability becomes a local catalogue-discovery and intervention-coverage problem rather than an exponential token-length problem. We formalize this transition with two propositions and one corollary. Proposition 1 is the worst-case-mode-wise negative result: no finite intervention dictionary covers every distinguishable failure mode of an unbounded domain. Corollary 1 is the inverse-discovery implication: the logarithmic upper bound on mode discovery cannot accommodate linearly more distinct tail modes without exponentially more observed hard-failure events. Proposition 2 is the positive patch-local result: under log active-mode exposure and head-heavy coverage, a sufficient per-hard-decision intervention budget grows polylogarithmically in sequence length and becomes domain-constant once the patch catalogue saturates. The framework relocates rather than dissolves long-context difficulty: where the number of hard decisions itself grows with task length, reliability remains hard; the contribution is to identify the on-axis intervention rather than to make those regimes easy.

</details>


### [261] [SAGE: A Novelty Gate for Efficient Memory Evolution in Agentic LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30711)
*Sijia Wang,Dhanajit Brahma,Ricardo Henao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出SAGE，一种基于球面自适应门控的记忆演化方法，将记忆写入控制建模为新奇性检测问题，通过von Mises-Fisher密度估计器和自适应阈值来决定新增、合并或忽略事实，在多个模型上显著降低延迟和成本，同时保持记忆质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工作更多关注检索和存储层面，缺乏对记忆写入（write-side）控制的原则性研究，而智能体LLM需要不断决策新提取事实是否应添加、合并到现有记忆或被忽略。

Method: 将记忆演化建模为新奇性检测问题，提出SAGE：使用基于von Mises-Fisher的密度估计器对记忆嵌入上的候选事实打分，并通过自适应阈值（跟踪记忆存储几何结构）将候选事实路由为ADD（新增）、NOOP（忽略）或不确定情况（交由LLM合并）。

Result: 在LoCoMo上，SAGE在全部7个开源权重大小模型对比中取得最佳平均token-F1；在GPT-4o-mini上，添加阶段API成本降低3.4倍，延迟降低2.5倍，评判得分差距极小。作为A-Mem的即插即用二进制门控，在5个模型上跳过约16-18%的LLM调用，质量变化极小。

Conclusion: 新奇性感知的写入控制是提高长期智能体记忆质量和系统效率的实用杠杆。

Abstract: Agentic LLMs must continuously decide whether newly extracted facts should be added, merged with existing memories, or ignored, yet prior work has focused more on retrieval and storage than on principled write-side control. We frame memory evolution as a novelty-detection problem and propose SAGE, a Spherical Adaptive Gate for memory Evolution that scores candidate facts with a von Mises-Fisher-based density estimator over memory embeddings and routes them with an adaptive threshold that tracks memory-store geometry. SAGE resolves clearly novel facts as ADD, clearly redundant facts as NOOP, and sends only uncertain cases to an LLM merge step, reducing expensive write-time reasoning. On LoCoMo, SAGE achieves the best average token-F1 against Mem0 on all seven open-weight backbone comparisons, while on GPT-4o-mini it reduces add-phase API cost by 3.4$\times$ and add-phase latency by 2.5$\times$ with only a small average judge-score gap. As a drop-in binary gate for A-Mem, SAGE skips roughly 16-18% of LLM calls across five models with minimal quality change on open-weight backbones. These results suggest that novelty-aware write control is a practical lever for improving both memory quality and system efficiency in long-term agentic memory.

### [262] [Pairwise Reference Alignment as a Model-Level Ordinal Observable](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30758)
*Mujing Li*

Main category: cs.CL

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的成对偏好数据广泛用于模型评估和对齐，但缺乏一个基础性的测量问题：当检验模型是否将偏好响应排在拒绝响应之上时，究竟估计的是什么样的模型级量？本文旨在填补这一概念和统计上的空白。

Method: 定义了成对参考对齐为模型排序与参考偏好排序一致的概率；提出了一个中心化的序参量统计量及其基于边界的扩展；给出了在独立采样假设下的有限样本估计量和集中界。

Result: 在Qwen2.5模型和RewardBench上的实验表明，所提出的统计量随模型规模和指令微调而增加，并且在不同参考对子集上的变化与理论预测一致。

Conclusion: 本文提供了一个清晰的成对参考对齐的概念和统计框架，区分了通用序数观测值与具体评分选择（如归一化log概率或基于能量的评分），为偏好数据的使用提供了更严谨的基础。

Abstract: Pairwise preference data is widely used in language-model evaluation and alignment, often for model ranking, reward modeling, or preference optimization. This note formulates a more basic measurement question: given a reference distribution of pairwise preferences, what model-level quantity is estimated when we test whether a model ranks preferred responses above rejected responses?
  We define pairwise reference alignment as an ordinal observable induced by a model scoring function. Given a reference pair distribution $P_{\mathrm{pair}}$ over triples $(x,y^+,y^-)$, and a scalar model score $S_M(x,y)$, we define the alignment observable as the probability that the model-induced ordering agrees with the reference preference ordering. We further define a centered order-parameter-like statistic and discuss a margin-based extension. The resulting quantities admit simple finite-sample estimators and concentration bounds under independent sampling assumptions.
  This note does not introduce a new benchmark. It provides a conceptual and statistical formulation for pairwise reference alignment, clarifies the role of the reference pair distribution, and distinguishes the general ordinal observable from scoring choices such as normalized log-probability or energy-based scores. We also provide an initial empirical study on Qwen2.5 models and RewardBench, where the proposed statistics increase with model size and instruction tuning and vary across reference-pair subsets as predicted by the formulation.

### [264] [Cognitive Fatigue in Autoregressive Transformers: Formalization and Measurement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30981)
*Riju Marwah,Ritvik Garimella,Vishal Pallagani,Atishay Jain,Michael Stewart,Amit Sheth*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出"认知疲劳"概念，将大语言模型在长文本生成中的退化现象形式化，并设计了一个轻量级的疲劳指数(Fatigue Index, FI)用于实时监控模型状态，实验表明FI能高效预测任务退化和重复生成等问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自回归语言模型在长文本生成中常出现重复文本、指令遵循能力下降、熵不稳定等退化现象，但缺乏在线诊断工具来实时检测这些失败。

Method: 提出Fatigue Index (FI)，聚合三个信号：对原始提示的注意力衰减、表征漂移、熵校准偏差，并满足单调性、有界性和可解释性三个公理。

Result: 在9个模型(1B-13B)上测试，FI预测任务退化AUROC=0.95，预测重复的Spearman rho=0.94；发现3B以下的指令微调模型比基础模型退化更快，7B时趋势反转；长上下文、中间位置证据和低精度会加速疲劳。

Abstract: Autoregressive language models frequently degrade during long-horizon generation, producing repetitive text, losing instruction adherence, and exhibiting unstable entropy. Despite the prevalence of these failures, practitioners lack online diagnostics to detect them in real-time as they occur. We formalize this degradation as cognitive fatigue, a measurable generation-time state characterized by decay in attention to the original prompt, representational drift, and entropy miscalibration. We introduce the Fatigue Index (FI), a lightweight, model-agnostic diagnostic that aggregates these three signals under explicit axioms (monotonicity, boundedness, interpretability) enabling reliable runtime monitoring. Across nine models (1B-13B parameters), FI trajectories exhibit structured temporal dynamics, predict task degradation (AUROC = 0.95) and repetition (Spearman rho = 0.94), and reveal non-monotonic scaling behavior: instruction-tuned models below 3B exhibit faster collapse than base models, with this trend reversing at 7B. Stress analyses further show that FI onset accelerates under longer contexts, middle-positioned evidence, and reduced numerical precision. These results establish cognitive fatigue as a coherent and measurable phenomenon, and position FI as a principled tool for runtime reliability monitoring in production LLM systems.

### [265] [Not All Synthetic Data Is Yours to Learn From](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31126)
*Sina Alemohammad,Li Chen,Richard G. Baraniuk,Zhangyang Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出"潜在能力浮现假说"：无提示、无监督的自训练能提升语言模型能力，但前提是合成数据与学生模型之间存在"兼容性"关系。研究发现自生成数据最有效，能力提升与记忆提取可解耦（在保持或提升基准性能的同时，逐字记忆提取率下降超95%）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究语言模型是否能在完全没有外部监督（无提示、无教师、无验证器、无奖励模型）的情况下，仅通过自身采样的文本进行自我改进，以及这种改进生效的条件。

Method: 在无提示的无条件自训练设定下，仅用BOS token生成文本对基础语言模型进行微调。通过对比不同数据源（自生成、同系列、跨系列）的训练效果，验证合成数据的效用是关系性的而非内在的。

Result: 1) 自生成数据最有效，同系列迁移优于更强但不同训练的数据，跨系列迁移最弱；2) 常见的内在代理指标（语义相似度、似然值）无法预测数据效用；3) 在Pythia实验中，能力提升与逐字记忆提取实现解耦，记忆提取率下降超95%而基准性能保持或提升。

Conclusion: 无提示自训练通过放大学生模型已具备的潜在能力（而非从数据中引入新结构）来生效，且该训练范式无需显式遗忘目标即可分离能力与记忆。

Abstract: Can a language model improve from plain text sampled from itself, with no prompts, no teacher, no verifier, and no reward model? Yes, but only when the synthetic corpus is compatible with the student, a relational property of the source-student pair rather than an intrinsic property of the data. We call this the latent capability resurfacing hypothesis: weak self-training can amplify capabilities already present in the pretrained model, but only under this compatibility condition. We study this in the minimal setting of prompt-free unconditional self-training, where base language models are fine-tuned on text generated from the BOS token alone, with no task specification or external supervision. We report three findings. First, synthetic utility is relational rather than intrinsic: self-generated data is the most effective source, same-lineage transfer outperforms stronger but differently trained sources, and cross-family transfer is substantially weaker. Second, common intrinsic proxies fail: neither benchmark-level semantic similarity nor average per-token likelihood under the student predicts which corpora help. Third, this regime produces a surprising byproduct. In controlled Pythia experiments, capability and verbatim memorization decouple: benchmark utility is preserved or improved while held-out exact-match extraction drops by over 95 percent, with no forget set, privacy objective, or targeted unlearning. Together, these results suggest that prompt-free self-training works by amplifying what the student already knows, not by importing structure from the data. They also reveal a regime in which capability and verbatim memorization can be separated without any explicit unlearning objective.

### [267] [Shared Doubt: Zero-shot Cross-Lingual Confidence Estimation for Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31220)
*Athina Kyriakou,Dennis Ulmer,Ivan Titov*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了多语言大模型是否编码了跨语言共享的置信度特征，通过轻量级线性探针在中间层捕获这些特征，实现零样本跨语言泛化，无需目标语言监督或重新训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有置信度估计方法多聚焦于英语，忽视了LLM的多语言使用场景，许多方法在不同语言间性能下降或需要重新训练。

Method: 使用轻量级线性探针（linear probe），从中间层表示中预测答案正确性。仅用单一语言训练，即可零样本泛化到未见过的、类型多样的语言。

Result: 探针在无目标语言监督下实现零样本跨语言泛化；置信度特征集中在模型中间层；跨语言性能与源语言相似度相关，但整体优于其他流行CE方法。

Conclusion: 多语言LLM存在一个共享的置信度子空间，位置在中间层。该方法无需重新训练即可作为跨语言置信度估计的强基线。

Abstract: Confidence estimation (CE), i.e. quantifying the reliability of a model's prediction, has attracted great interest in the context of large language models (LLMs). However, most studies focus on English, ignoring the multilingual reality of LLM usage, while many CE methods degrade or require retraining across languages. To address this gap, we investigate whether multilingual LLMs encode shared, language-transferable confidence features. We use a lightweight linear probe that predicts answer correctness directly from intermediate representations. Trained monolingually, the probe generalizes zero-shot to unseen, typologically diverse languages without target-language supervision. Learned layer weights and multiple ablations reveal that confidence features concentrate in middle layers across languages, suggesting a shared confidence subspace. While zero-shot cross-lingual performance depends on similarity to the source language, the probe provides a strong baseline without any retraining and compares favorably to other popular confidence estimation methods.

</details>


### [268] [Scaling Multi-Hop Training Data via Graph-Constrained Path Selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31238)
*Pengyu Chen,Yonggang Zhang,Mingming Chen,Jun Song,Wei Xue,Yike Guo*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出通过图约束（几何可容许性条件）从非结构化文本中离线枚举推理路径，再用教师模型将其转化为问答对，从而解决现有方法在模板化、密集交叉引用文档上性能退化的问题。在CUAD法律合同语料上，用8万条数据微调Qwen3-32B，Token F1从21.66%提升至38.58%。消融实验表明，增益主要来自语料扩展（4.4倍）而非单链质量提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法使用单一教师模型同时完成证据路径发现和问答对生成，在模板化、密集交叉引用的专业文档（如法律合同）中性能严重下降。需要一种能处理这类真实世界专业语料的多跳推理数据构造方法。

Method: 将推理路径发现与问答对生成解耦：(1) 离线在上下文关键词质心图上枚举推理路径，并通过5个几何可容许性约束（基于Gram矩阵论证，包括局部相似度界的端点漂移和上相似度界）进行过滤；(2) 仅用教师模型对已验证的路径进行问答对口头化。

Result: 在CUAD法律合同语料上微调Qwen3-32B（8万条数据），Token F1从21.66%提升至38.58%。消融实验表明，约束链与无约束链在同等训练规模下性能无显著差异，全部增益来自于语料规模扩展（4.4倍），即图约束的作用是提升教师模型的可合成性而非链质量。

Conclusion: 解耦推理路径枚举与问答对生成，并引入图几何约束，能有效从模板化、交叉引用密集的专业文档中构造高质量的多跳训练数据。增益机制是扩大了可用语料规模而非提升单链质量，这重新定义了图约束在该场景下的角色。

Abstract: Endowing large language models with compositional reasoning over specialized documents requires multi-hop training data at scale, where such data rarely exists outside of curated benchmarks built on structured sources. To construct it directly from plain, unannotated text, existing methods ask a single teacher model to jointly discover an evidence path through a document and verbalize it as a question-answer pair. However, these methods degrade sharply when documents are structured around repetitive templates and densely cross-referencing clauses, conditions that characterize most real-world specialized corpora. In this work, we decouple the two operations: reasoning paths are enumerated offline over a graph of contextual keyword centroids, and the teacher is invoked only to verbalize pre-validated paths. The graph enforces five geometric admissibility constraints, for which we provide Gram-matrix arguments establishing that local similarity bounds alone admit endpoint drift up to ${\sim}91^{\circ}$, and that an upper similarity bound is necessary to exit dense embedding cliques formed by boilerplate text. A matched-size ablation isolates the mechanism: at equal training scale, constrained and unconstrained chains yield indistinguishable downstream performance, and the gain at full scale comes from a 4.4$\times$ expansion of the usable corpus rather than from higher per-chain quality -- reframing the role of graph constraints, in this setting, as raising teacher synthesizability rather than improving chain content. Fine-tuning Qwen3-32B on 80K examples constructed from the CUAD legal contract corpus improves closed-book Token F1 from 21.66% to 38.58%. We have released our codes at https://github.com/hkgai-official/GCSCS.

### [269] [Skill Availability and Presentation Granularity in Large-Language-Model Agents: A Controlled SkillsBench Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31408)
*Xiaonan Xu,Wenjing Wu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究技能文档的呈现粒度（如抽象程度、是否包含工作示例）是否会显著影响大语言模型代理在下游任务中的表现，从而为技能知识的设计提供实证依据。

Method: 使用SkillsBench的30个任务子集，测试两种模型（GPT-5.5和DeepSeek V4-Flash），设置六种技能条件（无技能、不同抽象程度、有无工作示例等），每个条件重复5次试验，共收集1800条数据。通过配对对比和bootstrap置信区间评估效果。

Abstract: Skill documents provide procedural knowledge to large-language-model agents at inference time. This article studies whether the presentation granularity of controlled skill knowledge changes downstream task success. The experiment uses a pinned SkillsBench version, a 30-task domain-balanced subset validated by official oracle runs, two reasoning-enabled model configurations, six skill conditions, and five trials per task-condition-model cell. Skill availability is the clearest empirical signal. Relative to no skill, skill conditions increase task-mean pass rate by 26.7 to 36.0 percentage points for GPT-5.5 and by 18.0 to 26.0 percentage points for DeepSeek V4-Flash. The final data contain 1,800 rows, with 900 rows for each model. The task is the inference unit. Five trials are aggregated within each task-condition-model cell before paired contrasts are estimated over 30 tasks. The primary presentation contrasts are smaller and uncertain. Low-abstraction guidance differs from high-abstraction guidance by +0.7 percentage points for GPT-5.5 and -6.7 percentage points for DeepSeek V4-Flash, with both 95% bootstrap confidence intervals crossing zero. Adding one worked example to medium-abstraction guidance differs from the no-example variant by +0.7 and +1.3 percentage points. Mean-reward robustness checks preserve the same substantive conclusion. In this controlled subset, skill availability is associated with higher success than no skill, while the tested presentation-granularity changes yield small, uncertain, and model-dependent effects.

### [270] [Consolidating Rewarded Perturbations for LLM Post-Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31494)
*Zheyu Zhang,Shuo Yang,Gjergji Kasneci*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 提出CoRP方法，将奖励扰动种群合并为单一部署模型，无需推理时集成，在0.5B-8B模型和五个任务上平均提升8.1分，仅需一次前向传播。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法（如RandOpt）在推理时集成K个专家需要K次前向传播，且不适用于自由生成任务。作者希望将奖励种群压缩为单一模型，实现一次前向传播的部署。

Method: CoRP包含三个组件：奖励加权聚合、兼容性感知重加权、以及留出验证门控。该方法无需梯度计算，直接操作模型权重空间。

Result: 在五个语言模型（0.5B-8B）和五个任务上平均提升8.1分；使用RandOpt十分之一的扰动预算，超过单次推理RandOpt 6.5分，恢复50次多数投票集成的一半以上收益。

Conclusion: CoRP通过梯度自由的权重空间操作，有效将奖励种群合并为单一模型，在保持一次前向传播效率的同时取得显著性能提升。

Abstract: Post-training of language models is commonly framed as a sample-score-update loop implemented by gradient descent. A recent line of work, exemplified by RandOpt, relocates this loop to weight space, sampling Gaussian perturbations around a pretrained model and ensembling the top-K rewarded specialists at inference. While competitive with PPO and GRPO under matched training compute, this prediction-level ensemble incurs K forward passes per test example and does not extend cleanly to free-form generation. We ask whether the rewarded population can instead be folded into a single deployable model, replacing the inference-time ensemble with one consolidated update. A split-half analysis over 25 model-task pairs reveals reproducible low-rank structure in every case. We turn this geometry into CoRP (Consolidating Rewarded Perturbations), a gradient-free operator that combines reward-weighted aggregation, compatibility-aware reweighting, and a held-out validation gate, with no gradient flowing through the language model. Across five language models from 0.5B to 8B and five tasks covering math, code, and creative writing, CoRP improves the base model by 8.1 points on average. Using one tenth of RandOpt's perturbation budget, CoRP exceeds single-inference RandOpt by 6.5 points and recovers more than half of the gain of the 50-pass majority-vote ensemble, at one forward pass per test example.

### [271] [LongTraceRL: Learning Long-Context Reasoning from Search Agent Trajectories with Rubric Rewards](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31584)
*Nianyi Lin,Jiajie Zhang,Lei Hou,Juanzi Li*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: LongTraceRL提出通过知识图谱随机游走生成多跳问题，并利用搜索智能体轨迹构建高/低混淆度两级干扰物，同时设计基于实体级过程监督的细粒度奖励，显著提升了长上下文推理能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有强化学习方法受限于低混淆度干扰物和稀疏的最终结果奖励信号，无法监督中间推理步骤，导致模型在长上下文中难以定位和整合关键信息。

Method: 1) 数据构建：通过知识图谱随机游走生成多跳问题，利用搜索智能体轨迹构建两级干扰物（高混淆度：已读未引用文档；低混淆度：未打开文档）。2) 奖励设计：提出基于推理链上金实体的细粒度过程监督奖励（rubric reward），仅对正确答案响应应用（正样本策略），区分推理质量。

Result: 在4B-30B三个推理LLM上，五个长上下文基准测试中，LongTraceRL持续优于强基线方法。

Conclusion: LongTraceRL通过高质量干扰物构建和细粒度过程奖励，有效促进了全面、有证据支撑的长上下文推理。

Abstract: Long-context reasoning remains a central challenge for large language models, which often fail to locate and integrate key information in extensive distracting content. Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has shown promise for this task, yet existing methods are limited by low-confusability distractors and sparse, outcome-only reward signals that cannot supervise intermediate reasoning steps. To address these issues, we introduce \textsc{LongTraceRL}. For data construction, we generate multi-hop questions via knowledge graph random walks and leverage search agent trajectories to build \emph{tiered distractors}: documents the agent read but did not cite (high confusability) and documents that appeared in search results but were never opened (low confusability), producing training contexts that are far more challenging than those built by random sampling or one-shot search. For reward design, we propose a \emph{rubric reward} that uses the gold entities along each reasoning chain as fine-grained, entity-level process supervision. This rubric reward is applied only to responses with correct final answers (positive-only strategy), distinguishing the reasoning quality among correct responses and preventing reward hacking. Experiments on three reasoning LLMs (4B--30B) across five long-context benchmarks demonstrate that \textsc{LongTraceRL} consistently outperforms strong baselines and encourages comprehensive, evidence-grounded reasoning. Codes, datasets and models are available at \href{https://github.com/THU-KEG/LongTraceRL}{https://github.com/THU-KEG/LongTraceRL}.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

We evaluate MLIPilot on MACE potential optimization using both commercial and open-weight LLM agents, including GPT-5.5, GPT-4.1, Mistral-24B, and Qwen3-32B. The benchmarks span molecular and periodic settings: a QM7-derived dataset for which we generated B3LYP/6-31G(d) energies and forces, and a Cu EMT dataset with periodic copper supercells labeled by ASE's Effective Medium Theory calculator. Across these benchmarks, the strongest agents move initially constraint-violating baselines to accepted models by discovering useful training strategies, including output normalization, loss-function changes, progressive training schedules, and model-capacity adjustments. These results suggest that LLM agents can serve as autonomous operators for scientific machine-learning workflows when their search is constrained by domain-specific validation criteria, shifting part of MLIP development from manual trial-and-error toward auditable, automated experimentation.

### [274] [S$^3$LDBO: A Snapshot Single-Loop Algorithm for Decentralized Bilevel Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31311)
*Chao Yin,Youran Dong,Shiqian Ma,Bofan Wang,Junfeng Yang*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为Snapshot-SLDBO（S³LDBO）的单循环去中心化双层优化算法，通过快照机制允许智能体间歇性跳过昂贵的导数计算，在保持学习性能的同时提升计算效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 去中心化网络AI系统中，双层优化（如超参数优化、数据清洗、元学习）需要反复计算梯度、雅可比和海森矩阵，给单个智能体带来沉重计算负担。

Method: 提出Snapshot-SLDBO算法，采用单循环结构和快照机制，智能体可选择性地跳过昂贵导数计算，作为一种自主计算-适应策略，在保持全局协作学习的同时进行局部更新。

Result: 在超参数优化（合成和MNIST数据集）、数据超清洗（Fashion-MNIST）和去中心化元学习（miniImageNet）上验证，算法在保持竞争力的学习性能同时提升了计算效率。

Conclusion: 所提算法在确定性设置下建立了遍历迭代复杂度和高概率非遍历迭代复杂度，为去中心化双层优化提供了高效的计算方案。

Abstract: Networked AI systems increasingly rely on multiple agents that collaboratively learn and adapt models over communication networks. In such systems, bilevel formulations naturally arise in hyperparameter optimization, data cleaning, and meta-learning, but the repeated evaluation of gradients, Jacobians, and Hessians can impose a substantial computational burden on individual agents. To address this challenge, we propose Snapshot-SLDBO (S$^3$LDBO), an efficient single-loop decentralized bilevel optimization algorithm that enables agents to intermittently skip expensive derivative evaluations through a snapshot mechanism. This mechanism can be interpreted as an autonomous computation-adaptation strategy for networked AI, where agents selectively perform costly local updates while maintaining global collaborative learning. We establish the ergodic iteration complexity and the high probability nonergodic iteration complexity of the proposed algorithm within a deterministic setting. Experimental results on hyperparameter optimization with synthetic and MNIST datasets, data hyper-cleaning on Fashion-MNIST, and decentralized meta-learning on miniImageNet demonstrate that the proposed algorithm improves computational efficiency while maintaining competitive learning performance.

### [275] [A Unifying View of Anchoring via Operator-Side Tikhonov Regularization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30905)
*Zihao Chen*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文提出锚定（anchoring）方法可以统一看作在基础方法查询的算子中加入一个消失的Tikhonov正则项，然后运行未修改的基础方法。该框架解释了Halpern迭代、前向步、外梯度（EG）和过去外梯度（PEG）等方法的锚定机制，并给出了新的残差收敛保证和正则化变体。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有锚定变体虽然能实现尖锐的末次迭代保证，但从更新层面的角度看，锚点的放置方式因算法而异且在概念上不透明。作者希望找到一个统一的算子层面框架来解释锚定方法的本质。

Method: 提出一个统一的算子层面构造：在基础方法查询的算子中加入一个消失的Tikhonov正则项，然后直接运行未修改的基础方法。将这一配方分别应用于Picard迭代（得到Halpern迭代）、前向步、外梯度（EG）和过去外梯度（PEG），得到对应的锚定变体。

Result: 四种分析共享一个残差递推关系：恢复Halpern迭代的O(1/k)残差范数收敛率；正则化前向步得到O(1/√k)的收敛率；在无约束单调Lipschitz设定下，正则化EG和PEG变体均得到O(1/k)的收敛率。前向步实例还给出了新的残差收敛保证。

Conclusion: 锚定方法可以在算子层面通过Tikhonov正则化统一理解，为设计具有末次迭代保证的新算法提供了清晰的概念框架。

Abstract: Anchored fixed point and monotone equation methods, including Halpern iteration, extra anchored gradient, and their relatives, add a vanishing pull toward a reference point to obtain last-iterate guarantees. Existing anchored variants often achieve sharp last-iterate guarantees, but from the update-level perspective the placement of the anchor can be algorithm-specific and conceptually opaque. We show that anchoring admits a single operator-side construction: regularize the operator queried by the base method with a vanishing Tikhonov term, then run the unmodified base method. Applied to the Picard iteration, this recipe reproduces the Halpern iteration; applied to the forward step, extragradient (EG), and past extragradient (PEG, also known as Popov's method), it yields three variants whose anchor placements inherit the base method's query pattern. The forward-step instantiation gives a new residual convergence guarantee, while the EG and PEG instantiations give new regularized variants. The four analyses share a residual recurrence, recovering the $O(1/k)$ Halpern residual-norm convergence rate, giving $O(1/\sqrt{k})$ for the regularized forward step, and giving $O(1/k)$ for the regularized EG and PEG variants in the unconstrained monotone Lipschitz setting.

</details>


### [276] [Wall-Clock Complexity for Zeroth-Order Optimization with Tunable Oracle Fidelity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31346)
*Alexandra Suvorikova,Igor Pavlov,Artem Vasin,Georgii Bychkov,Anastasia Antsiferova,Darina Dvinskikh,Alexander Gasnikov*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文研究黑盒优化中可调精度oracle的代价权衡问题，提出一个精确感知的挂钟时间模型，推导了算法参数的最优选择，并发现加速方法可能在挂钟时间上劣于非加速方法，同时给出了恒精度策略最优的条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在零阶（黑盒）优化中，梯度不可用且目标评估依赖昂贵的仿真。许多应用中oracle的精度是可调的：高精度查询降低噪声但计算成本更高。现有研究缺乏统一的模型来捕捉这种精度-成本权衡，并指导实际参数选择。

Method: 提出一个精度感知的挂钟时间模型：每个精度δ的查询成本为c(δ)，总时间T_total = ∑c(δ_k)，需满足目标精度约束。通过分析oracle类型、噪声模型和优化方案，推导出挂钟时间最优的算法参数选择。

Result: 发现加速方法在挂钟时间上可能劣于非加速方案；刻画了恒精度策略在Big-O意义下最优的条件；提供了将收敛保证转化为实际精度和批量大小建议的统一方法论。

Conclusion: 本文为黑盒优化中可调精度oracle的代价-精度权衡提供了统一分析框架，揭示了实际部署中算法选择的新见解（如加速方法并非总是更优），并为实践者提供了参数调优的指导原则。

Abstract: Zeroth-order (black-box) optimization is applied when gradients are unavailable and objective evaluations rely on expensive simulations. In many such applications, the oracle fidelity is tunable: higher-accuracy queries reduce noise but incur higher computational costs. To capture this trade-off, we study an accuracy-aware wall-clock model where each query with fidelity $δ$ has a cost $c(δ)$, and we minimize the total time $T_{\mathrm{total}} = \sum_{k=1}^{N} c(δ_k)$, subject to a target accuracy constraint. We show how the choice of oracle type, noise model, and optimization scheme induces explicit wall-clock-optimal choices for the algorithmic parameters. For instance, we demonstrate that accelerated methods can be wall-clock inferior to non-accelerated schemes. Furthermore, we characterize the conditions under which a constant fidelity strategy is optimal in the Big-O sense. Our framework provides a unified methodology to translate convergence guarantees into practical fidelity and batching recommendations.

</details>


<div id='cs.HC'></div>

# cs.HC [[Back]](#toc)

### [277] [Rationalize: Shared Semantic Reasoning for Human-AI Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.30632)
*Aritra Dasgupta,Naga Datha Saikiran Battula,Avina Nakarmi,Sohom Sen,Subhodeep Ghosh,Xun Song*

Main category: cs.HC

TL;DR: 提出Rationalize框架，通过四组互补角色对（探索者-引导者、调查者-信息提供者、教师-学生、法官-倡导者）在共享推理空间中实现人机双向对齐与语义推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的人机交互研究多聚焦于输出层面的对齐，缺乏对推理过程和意图层面的共享语义理解。论文旨在弥合这一鸿沟，让人类与AI不仅结果对齐，更在推理层面实现双向理解。

Method: 基于人机协作和批判性思维理论，提出角色对（Role-Pair）框架Rationalize，将人机交互定义为Explorer-Guide、Investigator-Informant、Teacher-Student、Judge-Advocate四组互补角色对，在共享推理空间中明确目的、问题、假设、证据、推理和影响。

Result: 将角色对映射到双向人机对齐框架（"AI对齐人类"与"人类对齐AI"），展示了不同角色下对齐方向的差异，并提出了基于要素级和角色特定方法的对齐设计与评估研究议程。

Conclusion: Rationalize框架为人机在推理层面的共享语义理解提供了结构化的角色设计，为未来人机对齐研究提供了协作研究路线图。

Abstract: We introduce Rationalize, a role-pair framework for shared semantic reasoning between humans and AI models in data-driven sensemaking. Building on ideas in human-machine teaming and critical thinking, we conceptualize human-AI interaction as a series of complementary role pairs (Explorer-Guide, Investigator-Informant, Teacher-Student, Judge-Advocate) operating in a shared reasoning space. In this space, human analysts and AI models (such as LLMs) make purposes, questions, assumptions, evidence, inferences, and implications explicit, facilitating alignment not only at the output level but at the level of rationalization of intent and action by each side. We relate these role pairs to the bidirectional human-AI alignment framework, illustrating how "aligning AI to humans" and "aligning humans to AI" differ by role, and sketch a collaborative research agenda for alignment design and assessment using element-level and role-specific approaches.

</details>
